						var securePrefix = "secure."
						domain = (h == "localhost" ?  null : "." + (h.indexOf(securePrefix) == 0 ? h.substr(securePrefix.length+(securePrefix.indexOf(".") != -1 ? 0 : 1)) : h));

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openFooterAtTop(url,linkNum){
		var footerCIDNum = "1095919";
		var MLINK = (url.indexOf('?') != -1) && (url.substring(url.indexOf('?')).length > 2) ? "&mlink=5058," : "?mlink=5058,";
		var tmp = url + MLINK + footerCIDNum + "," + linkNum + "&clink=" + footerCIDNum;
		top.location.href = tmp;
		return false;
	}
	
// FEDEX TRACKING	
(function() {
    if (location.pathname == "/profile/shipment_detail.do") {
        Event.onDOMReady(function() {
            var as = $$('a[href*=http://fedex.com/Tracking?action=track&language=english&cntry_code=us&initial=x&tracknumbers]');
            as.each(function(a){
                if (a && a.href) {
                    var url = a.href;
                    if (url.indexOf("tracknumbers=") == -1) {
                        url = url.replace("tracknumbers","tracknumbers=");
                        a.href = url;
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
})();

		var obj1095919 = new Object();

		obj1095919.qryString = String(obj1095919.qry);
		obj1095919.aQry = obj1095919.qryString.indexOf('kwid=1');
		
		if (obj1095919.aQry < 0){
		var piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 = (getCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop") == 1);
			if (piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 != 1) {
				plGapPromoPop = window.open('/browse/info.do?cid=36193','Piperlime','width=365,height=262,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100');
					if (plGapPromoPop) {

    Event.observe(window,'load', fireOmni);

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openFooterAtTop(url,linkNum){
		var footerCIDNum = "1095919";
		var MLINK = (url.indexOf('?') != -1) && (url.substring(url.indexOf('?')).length > 2) ? "&mlink=5058," : "?mlink=5058,";
		var tmp = url + MLINK + footerCIDNum + "," + linkNum + "&clink=" + footerCIDNum;
		top.location.href = tmp;
		return false;
	}
	
// FEDEX TRACKING	
(function() {
    if (location.pathname == "/profile/shipment_detail.do") {
        Event.onDOMReady(function() {
            var as = $$('a[href*=http://fedex.com/Tracking?action=track&language=english&cntry_code=us&initial=x&tracknumbers]');
            as.each(function(a){
                if (a && a.href) {
                    var url = a.href;
                    if (url.indexOf("tracknumbers=") == -1) {
                        url = url.replace("tracknumbers","tracknumbers=");
                        a.href = url;
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
})();

	
	
// PIPERLIME POPUNDER	
	function openPiperlime1095919() {
		var obj1095919 = new Object();
		
		obj1095919.qry = location;
		obj1095919.qryString = String(obj1095919.qry);
		obj1095919.aQry = obj1095919.qryString.indexOf('kwid=1');
		
		if (obj1095919.aQry < 0){
		var piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 = (getCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop") == 1);
			if (piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 != 1) {
				plGapPromoPop = window.open('/browse/info.do?cid=36193','Piperlime','width=365,height=262,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100');
					if (plGapPromoPop) {
						plGapPromoPop.blur();
						window.focus();
						setCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop","1");				
					}
			}
		
		}
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openFooterAtTop(url,linkNum){
		var footerCIDNum = "1095919";
		var MLINK = (url.indexOf('?') != -1) && (url.substring(url.indexOf('?')).length > 2) ? "&mlink=5058," : "?mlink=5058,";
		var tmp = url + MLINK + footerCIDNum + "," + linkNum + "&clink=" + footerCIDNum;
		top.location.href = tmp;
		return false;
	}
	
// FEDEX TRACKING	
(function() {
    if (location.pathname == "/profile/shipment_detail.do") {
        Event.onDOMReady(function() {
            var as = $$('a[href*=http://fedex.com/Tracking?action=track&language=english&cntry_code=us&initial=x&tracknumbers]');
            as.each(function(a){
                if (a && a.href) {
                    var url = a.href;
                    if (url.indexOf("tracknumbers=") == -1) {
                        url = url.replace("tracknumbers","tracknumbers=");
                        a.href = url;
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
})();

	
	
// PIPERLIME POPUNDER	
	function openPiperlime1095919() {
		var obj1095919 = new Object();
		
		obj1095919.qry = location;
		obj1095919.qryString = String(obj1095919.qry);
		obj1095919.aQry = obj1095919.qryString.indexOf('kwid=1');
		
		if (obj1095919.aQry < 0){
		var piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 = (getCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop") == 1);
			if (piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 != 1) {
				plGapPromoPop = window.open('/browse/info.do?cid=36193','Piperlime','width=365,height=262,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100');
					if (plGapPromoPop) {
						plGapPromoPop.blur();
						window.focus();
						setCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop","1");				
					}
			}
		
		}
	}

// <![CDATA[
		
			
				
				   if(!(location.protocol == "https:")){
						var h = location.hostname;
						var securePrefix = "secure."
						domain = (h == "localhost" ?  null : "." + (h.indexOf(securePrefix) == 0 ? h.substr(securePrefix.length+(securePrefix.indexOf(".") != -1 ? 0 : 1)) : h));

					  index = domain.lastIndexOf (":");
					  if(index > 0){
					  	domain = domain.substring(0,index);
					  }
         			  domain = "." + domain;
					}
					deleteDomainCookies(domain);
				
			
		

 // ]]>	
 </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openFooterAtTop(url,linkNum){
		var footerCIDNum = "1095919";
		var MLINK = (url.indexOf('?') != -1) && (url.substring(url.indexOf('?')).length > 2) ? "&mlink=5058," : "?mlink=5058,";
		var tmp = url + MLINK + footerCIDNum + "," + linkNum + "&clink=" + footerCIDNum;
		top.location.href = tmp;
		return false;
	}
	
// FEDEX TRACKING	
(function() {
    if (location.pathname == "/profile/shipment_detail.do") {
        Event.onDOMReady(function() {
            var as = $$('a[href*=http://fedex.com/Tracking?action=track&language=english&cntry_code=us&initial=x&tracknumbers]');
            as.each(function(a){
                if (a && a.href) {
                    var url = a.href;
                    if (url.indexOf("tracknumbers=") == -1) {
                        url = url.replace("tracknumbers","tracknumbers=");
                        a.href = url;
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
})();

	
	
// PIPERLIME POPUNDER	
	function openPiperlime1095919() {
		var obj1095919 = new Object();
		
		obj1095919.qry = location;
		obj1095919.qryString = String(obj1095919.qry);
		obj1095919.aQry = obj1095919.qryString.indexOf('kwid=1');
		
		if (obj1095919.aQry < 0){
		var piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 = (getCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop") == 1);
			if (piperlimePopHasSeen1095919 != 1) {
				plGapPromoPop = window.open('/browse/info.do?cid=36193','Piperlime','width=365,height=262,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100');
					if (plGapPromoPop) {
						plGapPromoPop.blur();
						window.focus();
						setCookieVar("mktGlobalPersist","plGapPromoPop","1");				
					}
			}
		
		}
	}

	Event.observe(window, 'load', openPiperlime1095919);

		thisBrowser = navigator.userAgent;

		var MLINK = (url.indexOf('?') != -1) && (url.substring(url.indexOf('?')).length > 2) ? "&mlink=5058," : "?mlink=5058,";
		var tmp = url + MLINK + footerCIDNum + "," + linkNum + "&clink=" + footerCIDNum;
		top.location.href = tmp;
		return false;
	}
	
// FEDEX TRACKING	
(function() {
    if (location.pathname == "/profile/shipment_detail.do") {
        Event.onDOMReady(function() {
            var as = $$('a[href*=http://fedex.com/Tracking?action=track&language=english&cntry_code=us&initial=x&tracknumbers]');
            as.each(function(a){
                if (a && a.href) {
                    var url = a.href;
                    if (url.indexOf("tracknumbers=") == -1) {
                        url = url.replace("tracknumbers","tracknumbers=");
                        a.href = url;
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }
})();

		}
	}
